         "export class Maybe {\n    constructor(value) {\n        this.value = value;\n    }\n    static from(value) {\n        return new Maybe(value);\n    }\n    static of(value) {\n        return new Maybe(value);\n    }\n    static nothing() {\n        return new Maybe();\n    }\n    static equals(lhv, rhv) {\n        return lhv.inner() === rhv.inner();\n    }\n    isJust() {\n        return !this.isNothing();\n    }\n    isNothing() {\n        return this.value === undefined;\n    }\n    map(fn) {\n        if (this.isNothing()) {\n            return new Maybe();\n        }\n        return new Maybe(fn(this.value));\n    }\n    chain(fn) {\n        if (this.isNothing()) {\n            return new Maybe();\n        }\n        return fn(this.value);\n    }\n    asyncChain(fn) {\n        if (this.isNothing()) {\n            return Promise.resolve(new Maybe());\n        }\n        return fn(this.value);\n    }\n    unwrap() {\n        if (this.isNothing()) {\n            throw new Error('Nothing to unwrap');\n        }\n        return this.value;\n    }\n    inner() {\n        return this.value;\n    }\n}\n",
